<s> the stroke had indeed slipped past their defences into the very wood of their tree <\s>

<s> thought young jolyon soundest timber of our land <\s>

<s> in their hearts they would even feel it an intervention of providence a retribution had not bosinney endangered their two most priceless possessions the pocket and the hearth <\s>
<s> and they would talk of that unfortunate accident of young bosinney's but perhaps they would not talk silence might be better <\s>
<s> as for himself he regarded the bus driver's account of the accident as of very little value <\s>

<s> and so he too rejected this theory of suicide the dead man's face rose too clearly before him <\s>

<s> chapter ix irene's return after leaving james and old jolyon in the mortuary of the hospital soames hurried aimlessly along the streets <\s>

<s> this had given him time to breathe time to leave no stone unturned to find her <\s>
<s> but now cut off from taking steps by bosinney's death that strange death to think of which was like putting a hot iron to his heart like lifting a great weight from it he did not know how to pass his day and he wandered here and there through the streets looking at every face he met devoured by a hundred anxieties <\s>
<s> and as he wandered he thought of him who had finished his wandering his prowling and would never haunt his house again <\s>

<s> this had given him time to breathe time to leave no stone unturned to find her <\s>
<s> but now cut off from taking steps by bosinney's death that strange death to think of which was like putting a hot iron to his heart like lifting a great weight from it he did not know how to pass his day and he wandered here and there through the streets looking at every face he met devoured by a hundred anxieties <\s>
<s> and as he wandered he thought of him who had finished his wandering his prowling and would never haunt his house again <\s>
<s> already in the afternoon he passed posters announcing the identity of the dead man and bought the papers to see what they said <\s>
<s> he would stop their mouths if he could and he went into the city and was closeted with boulter for a long time <\s>
<s> on his way home passing the steps of jobson's about half past four he met george forsyte who held out an evening paper to soames saying here <\s>
<s> have you seen this about the poor buccaneer <\s>
<s> soames answered stonily yes <\s>
<s> george stared at him <\s>
<s> he had never liked soames he now held him responsible for bosinney's death <\s>
<s> and the thought of how to keep june's name out of the business kept whirring in his brain <\s>
<s> james had his son to support him <\s>
<s> why should he not send for jo <\s>
<s> taking out his card case he pencilled the following message come round at once <\s>

<s> jolyon forsyte were there to give him the card and bring him at once <\s>
<s> if not there yet he was to wait till he came <\s>

<s> but take your time <\s>

<s> with a huge steady hand the inspector took the hem and turned it back <\s>
<s> a sightless face gazed up at them and on either side of that sightless defiant face the three forsytes gazed down in each one of them the secret emotions fears and pity of his own nature rose and fell like the rising falling waves of life whose wash those white walls barred out now for ever from bosinney <\s>
<s> and in each one of them the trend of his nature the odd essential spring which moved him in fashions minutely unalterably different from those of every other human being forced him to a different attitude of thought <\s>
<s> far from the others yet inscrutably close each stood thus alone with death silent his eyes lowered <\s>
<s> the inspector asked softly you identify the gentleman sir <\s>
<s> old jolyon raised his head and nodded <\s>
<s> he looked at his brother opposite at that long lean figure brooding over the dead man with face dusky red and strained grey eyes and at the figure of soames white and still by his father's side <\s>
<s> and all that he had felt against those two was gone like smoke in the long white presence of death <\s>

<s> sudden reverse of all that goes before blind setting forth on a path that leads to where <\s>
<s> dark quenching of the fire <\s>

<s> you'll come to me as soon as you can jo and with his head bowed he went away <\s>

<s> the stroke had fallen too swiftly <\s>

<s> or so at all events young jolyon seemed to see them lying around bosinney's body <\s>
<s> he asked the inspector to tell him what had happened and the latter like a man who does not every day get such a chance again detailed such facts as were known <\s>
<s> there's more here sir however he said than meets the eye <\s>
<s> i don't believe in suicide nor in pure accident myself <\s>

<s> he walked sorrowfully away from the hospital towards his father's house reflecting that this death would break up the forsyte family <\s>
<s> the stroke had indeed slipped past their defences into the very wood of their tree <\s>
<s> they might flourish to all appearance as before preserving a brave show before the eyes of london but the trunk was dead withered by the same flash that had stricken down bosinney <\s>
<s> and now the saplings would take its place each one a new custodian of the sense of property <\s>
<s> good forest of forsytes <\s>
<s> thought young jolyon soundest timber of our land <\s>
<s> concerning the cause of this death his family would doubtless reject with vigour the suspicion of suicide which was so compromising <\s>
<s> they would take it as an accident a stroke of fate <\s>
<s> in their hearts they would even feel it an intervention of providence a retribution had not bosinney endangered their two most priceless possessions the pocket and the hearth <\s>
<s> and they would talk of that unfortunate accident of young bosinney's but perhaps they would not talk silence might be better <\s>
<s> as for himself he regarded the bus driver's account of the accident as of very little value <\s>
<s> for no one so madly in love committed suicide for want of money nor was bosinney the sort of fellow to set much store by a financial crisis <\s>
<s> and so he too rejected this theory of suicide the dead man's face rose too clearly before him <\s>

<s> chapter ix irene's return after leaving james and old jolyon in the mortuary of the hospital soames hurried aimlessly along the streets <\s>
<s> the tragic event of bosinney's death altered the complexion of everything <\s>
<s> there was no longer the same feeling that to lose a minute would be fatal nor would he now risk communicating the fact of his wife's flight to anyone till the inquest was over <\s>
<s> that morning he had risen early before the postman came had taken the first post letters from the box himself and though there had been none from irene he had made an opportunity of telling bilson that her mistress was at the sea he would probably he said be going down himself from saturday to monday <\s>
<s> this had given him time to breathe time to leave no stone unturned to find her <\s>
<s> but now cut off from taking steps by bosinney's death that strange death to think of which was like putting a hot iron to his heart like lifting a great weight from it he did not know how to pass his day and he wandered here and there through the streets looking at every face he met devoured by a hundred anxieties <\s>
<s> and as he wandered he thought of him who had finished his wandering his prowling and would never haunt his house again <\s>
<s> already in the afternoon he passed posters announcing the identity of the dead man and bought the papers to see what they said <\s>
<s> he would stop their mouths if he could and he went into the city and was closeted with boulter for a long time <\s>
<s> on his way home passing the steps of jobson's about half past four he met george forsyte who held out an evening paper to soames saying here <\s>
<s> have you seen this about the poor buccaneer <\s>
<s> soames answered stonily yes <\s>
<s> george stared at him <\s>
<s> he had never liked soames he now held him responsible for bosinney's death <\s>

<s> if not there yet he was to wait till he came <\s>

<s> but take your time <\s>

<s> with a huge steady hand the inspector took the hem and turned it back <\s>
<s> a sightless face gazed up at them and on either side of that sightless defiant face the three forsytes gazed down in each one of them the secret emotions fears and pity of his own nature rose and fell like the rising falling waves of life whose wash those white walls barred out now for ever from bosinney <\s>
<s> and in each one of them the trend of his nature the odd essential spring which moved him in fashions minutely unalterably different from those of every other human being forced him to a different attitude of thought <\s>
<s> far from the others yet inscrutably close each stood thus alone with death silent his eyes lowered <\s>
<s> the inspector asked softly you identify the gentleman sir <\s>
<s> old jolyon raised his head and nodded <\s>
<s> he looked at his brother opposite at that long lean figure brooding over the dead man with face dusky red and strained grey eyes and at the figure of soames white and still by his father's side <\s>

<s> the stroke had indeed slipped past their defences into the very wood of their tree <\s>
<s> they might flourish to all appearance as before preserving a brave show before the eyes of london but the trunk was dead withered by the same flash that had stricken down bosinney <\s>
<s> and now the saplings would take its place each one a new custodian of the sense of property <\s>
<s> good forest of forsytes <\s>
<s> thought young jolyon soundest timber of our land <\s>
<s> concerning the cause of this death his family would doubtless reject with vigour the suspicion of suicide which was so compromising <\s>
<s> they would take it as an accident a stroke of fate <\s>
<s> in their hearts they would even feel it an intervention of providence a retribution had not bosinney endangered their two most priceless possessions the pocket and the hearth <\s>
<s> and they would talk of that unfortunate accident of young bosinney's but perhaps they would not talk silence might be better <\s>
<s> as for himself he regarded the bus driver's account of the accident as of very little value <\s>
<s> for no one so madly in love committed suicide for want of money nor was bosinney the sort of fellow to set much store by a financial crisis <\s>
<s> and so he too rejected this theory of suicide the dead man's face rose too clearly before him <\s>
<s> gone in the heyday of his summer and to believe thus that an accident had cut bosinney off in the full sweep of his passion was more than ever pitiful to young jolyon <\s>
<s> then came a vision of soames home as it now was and must be hereafter <\s>
<s> the streak of lightning had flashed its clear uncanny gleam on bare bones with grinning spaces between the disguising flesh was gone .... <\s>

<s> he looked very wan in his great armchair <\s>

<s> he said is that you <\s>
<s> i've told poor little june <\s>
<s> but that's not all of it <\s>
<s> are you going to soames <\s>
<s> she's brought it on herself i suppose but somehow i can't bear to think of her shut up there and all alone <\s>
<s> and holding up his thin veined hand he clenched it <\s>
<s> chapter ix irene's return after leaving james and old jolyon in the mortuary of the hospital soames hurried aimlessly along the streets <\s>
<s> the tragic event of bosinney's death altered the complexion of everything <\s>
<s> there was no longer the same feeling that to lose a minute would be fatal nor would he now risk communicating the fact of his wife's flight to anyone till the inquest was over <\s>
<s> that morning he had risen early before the postman came had taken the first post letters from the box himself and though there had been none from irene he had made an opportunity of telling bilson that her mistress was at the sea he would probably he said be going down himself from saturday to monday <\s>
<s> this had given him time to breathe time to leave no stone unturned to find her <\s>
<s> but now cut off from taking steps by bosinney's death that strange death to think of which was like putting a hot iron to his heart like lifting a great weight from it he did not know how to pass his day and he wandered here and there through the streets looking at every face he met devoured by a hundred anxieties <\s>
<s> and as he wandered he thought of him who had finished his wandering his prowling and would never haunt his house again <\s>
<s> already in the afternoon he passed posters announcing the identity of the dead man and bought the papers to see what they said <\s>
<s> he would stop their mouths if he could and he went into the city and was closeted with boulter for a long time <\s>
<s> on his way home passing the steps of jobson's about half past four he met george forsyte who held out an evening paper to soames saying here <\s>
<s> have you seen this about the poor buccaneer <\s>
<s> soames answered stonily yes <\s>
<s> george stared at him <\s>
<s> he had never liked soames he now held him responsible for bosinney's death <\s>
<s> and the thought of how to keep june's name out of the business kept whirring in his brain <\s>
<s> james had his son to support him <\s>
<s> why should he not send for jo <\s>
<s> taking out his card case he pencilled the following message come round at once <\s>
<s> i've sent the carriage for you <\s>
<s> on getting out he gave this card to his coachman telling him to drive as fast as possible to the hotch potch club and if mr <\s>
<s> jolyon forsyte were there to give him the card and bring him at once <\s>
<s> if not there yet he was to wait till he came <\s>
<s> he followed the others slowly up the steps leaning on his umbrella and stood a moment to get his breath <\s>
<s> the inspector said this is the mortuary sir <\s>
<s> but take your time <\s>
<s> in the bare white walled room empty of all but a streak of sunshine smeared along the dustless floor lay a form covered by a sheet <\s>
<s> with a huge steady hand the inspector took the hem and turned it back <\s>
<s> a sightless face gazed up at them and on either side of that sightless defiant face the three forsytes gazed down in each one of them the secret emotions fears and pity of his own nature rose and fell like the rising falling waves of life whose wash those white walls barred out now for ever from bosinney <\s>
<s> and in each one of them the trend of his nature the odd essential spring which moved him in fashions minutely unalterably different from those of every other human being forced him to a different attitude of thought <\s>
<s> far from the others yet inscrutably close each stood thus alone with death silent his eyes lowered <\s>
<s> the inspector asked softly you identify the gentleman sir <\s>
<s> old jolyon raised his head and nodded <\s>
<s> he looked at his brother opposite at that long lean figure brooding over the dead man with face dusky red and strained grey eyes and at the figure of soames white and still by his father's side <\s>
<s> and all that he had felt against those two was gone like smoke in the long white presence of death <\s>

<s> sudden reverse of all that goes before blind setting forth on a path that leads to where <\s>
<s> dark quenching of the fire <\s>

<s> small and of no import insects though they are <\s>

<s> i'd better be going <\s>
<s> you'll come to me as soon as you can jo and with his head bowed he went away <\s>

<s> the stroke had indeed slipped past their defences into the very wood of their tree <\s>

<s> thought young jolyon soundest timber of our land <\s>

<s> in their hearts they would even feel it an intervention of providence a retribution had not bosinney endangered their two most priceless possessions the pocket and the hearth <\s>
<s> and they would talk of that unfortunate accident of young bosinney's but perhaps they would not talk silence might be better <\s>
<s> as for himself he regarded the bus driver's account of the accident as of very little value <\s>

<s> chapter ix irene's return after leaving james and old jolyon in the mortuary of the hospital soames hurried aimlessly along the streets <\s>
<s> the tragic event of bosinney's death altered the complexion of everything <\s>
<s> there was no longer the same feeling that to lose a minute would be fatal nor would he now risk communicating the fact of his wife's flight to anyone till the inquest was over <\s>
<s> that morning he had risen early before the postman came had taken the first post letters from the box himself and though there had been none from irene he had made an opportunity of telling bilson that her mistress was at the sea he would probably he said be going down himself from saturday to monday <\s>
<s> this had given him time to breathe time to leave no stone unturned to find her <\s>
<s> but now cut off from taking steps by bosinney's death that strange death to think of which was like putting a hot iron to his heart like lifting a great weight from it he did not know how to pass his day and he wandered here and there through the streets looking at every face he met devoured by a hundred anxieties <\s>
<s> and as he wandered he thought of him who had finished his wandering his prowling and would never haunt his house again <\s>
<s> already in the afternoon he passed posters announcing the identity of the dead man and bought the papers to see what they said <\s>
<s> he would stop their mouths if he could and he went into the city and was closeted with boulter for a long time <\s>
<s> on his way home passing the steps of jobson's about half past four he met george forsyte who held out an evening paper to soames saying here <\s>
<s> have you seen this about the poor buccaneer <\s>
<s> soames answered stonily yes <\s>
<s> george stared at him <\s>
<s> he had never liked soames he now held him responsible for bosinney's death <\s>

<s> if not there yet he was to wait till he came <\s>

<s> and in each one of them the trend of his nature the odd essential spring which moved him in fashions minutely unalterably different from those of every other human being forced him to a different attitude of thought <\s>
<s> far from the others yet inscrutably close each stood thus alone with death silent his eyes lowered <\s>

<s> old jolyon raised his head and nodded <\s>

<s> chapter ix irene's return after leaving james and old jolyon in the mortuary of the hospital soames hurried aimlessly along the streets <\s>
<s> the tragic event of bosinney's death altered the complexion of everything <\s>
<s> there was no longer the same feeling that to lose a minute would be fatal nor would he now risk communicating the fact of his wife's flight to anyone till the inquest was over <\s>
<s> that morning he had risen early before the postman came had taken the first post letters from the box himself and though there had been none from irene he had made an opportunity of telling bilson that her mistress was at the sea he would probably he said be going down himself from saturday to monday <\s>
<s> this had given him time to breathe time to leave no stone unturned to find her <\s>
<s> but now cut off from taking steps by bosinney's death that strange death to think of which was like putting a hot iron to his heart like lifting a great weight from it he did not know how to pass his day and he wandered here and there through the streets looking at every face he met devoured by a hundred anxieties <\s>
<s> and as he wandered he thought of him who had finished his wandering his prowling and would never haunt his house again <\s>
<s> already in the afternoon he passed posters announcing the identity of the dead man and bought the papers to see what they said <\s>
<s> he would stop their mouths if he could and he went into the city and was closeted with boulter for a long time <\s>
<s> on his way home passing the steps of jobson's about half past four he met george forsyte who held out an evening paper to soames saying here <\s>
<s> have you seen this about the poor buccaneer <\s>
<s> soames answered stonily yes <\s>
<s> george stared at him <\s>
<s> he had never liked soames he now held him responsible for bosinney's death <\s>

<s> and in each one of them the trend of his nature the odd essential spring which moved him in fashions minutely unalterably different from those of every other human being forced him to a different attitude of thought <\s>

<s> the stroke had indeed slipped past their defences into the very wood of their tree <\s>

<s> and now the saplings would take its place each one a new custodian of the sense of property <\s>
<s> good forest of forsytes <\s>
<s> thought young jolyon soundest timber of our land <\s>
<s> concerning the cause of this death his family would doubtless reject with vigour the suspicion of suicide which was so compromising <\s>
<s> they would take it as an accident a stroke of fate <\s>
<s> in their hearts they would even feel it an intervention of providence a retribution had not bosinney endangered their two most priceless possessions the pocket and the hearth <\s>
<s> and they would talk of that unfortunate accident of young bosinney's but perhaps they would not talk silence might be better <\s>
<s> as for himself he regarded the bus driver's account of the accident as of very little value <\s>
<s> for no one so madly in love committed suicide for want of money nor was bosinney the sort of fellow to set much store by a financial crisis <\s>
<s> and so he too rejected this theory of suicide the dead man's face rose too clearly before him <\s>

<s> chapter ix irene's return after leaving james and old jolyon in the mortuary of the hospital soames hurried aimlessly along the streets <\s>
<s> the tragic event of bosinney's death altered the complexion of everything <\s>
<s> there was no longer the same feeling that to lose a minute would be fatal nor would he now risk communicating the fact of his wife's flight to anyone till the inquest was over <\s>
<s> that morning he had risen early before the postman came had taken the first post letters from the box himself and though there had been none from irene he had made an opportunity of telling bilson that her mistress was at the sea he would probably he said be going down himself from saturday to monday <\s>
<s> this had given him time to breathe time to leave no stone unturned to find her <\s>
<s> but now cut off from taking steps by bosinney's death that strange death to think of which was like putting a hot iron to his heart like lifting a great weight from it he did not know how to pass his day and he wandered here and there through the streets looking at every face he met devoured by a hundred anxieties <\s>
<s> and as he wandered he thought of him who had finished his wandering his prowling and would never haunt his house again <\s>
<s> already in the afternoon he passed posters announcing the identity of the dead man and bought the papers to see what they said <\s>
<s> he would stop their mouths if he could and he went into the city and was closeted with boulter for a long time <\s>
<s> on his way home passing the steps of jobson's about half past four he met george forsyte who held out an evening paper to soames saying here <\s>
<s> have you seen this about the poor buccaneer <\s>

<s> george stared at him <\s>

<s> and in each one of them the trend of his nature the odd essential spring which moved him in fashions minutely unalterably different from those of every other human being forced him to a different attitude of thought <\s>
<s> far from the others yet inscrutably close each stood thus alone with death silent his eyes lowered <\s>

<s> old jolyon raised his head and nodded <\s>

<s> there's more here sir however he said than meets the eye <\s>

<s> the stroke had indeed slipped past their defences into the very wood of their tree <\s>
<s> they might flourish to all appearance as before preserving a brave show before the eyes of london but the trunk was dead withered by the same flash that had stricken down bosinney <\s>
<s> and now the saplings would take its place each one a new custodian of the sense of property <\s>
<s> good forest of forsytes <\s>
<s> thought young jolyon soundest timber of our land <\s>
<s> concerning the cause of this death his family would doubtless reject with vigour the suspicion of suicide which was so compromising <\s>
<s> they would take it as an accident a stroke of fate <\s>
<s> in their hearts they would even feel it an intervention of providence a retribution had not bosinney endangered their two most priceless possessions the pocket and the hearth <\s>
<s> and they would talk of that unfortunate accident of young bosinney's but perhaps they would not talk silence might be better <\s>
<s> as for himself he regarded the bus driver's account of the accident as of very little value <\s>
<s> for no one so madly in love committed suicide for want of money nor was bosinney the sort of fellow to set much store by a financial crisis <\s>
<s> and so he too rejected this theory of suicide the dead man's face rose too clearly before him <\s>
<s> gone in the heyday of his summer and to believe thus that an accident had cut bosinney off in the full sweep of his passion was more than ever pitiful to young jolyon <\s>

<s> chapter ix irene's return after leaving james and old jolyon in the mortuary of the hospital soames hurried aimlessly along the streets <\s>
<s> the tragic event of bosinney's death altered the complexion of everything <\s>
<s> there was no longer the same feeling that to lose a minute would be fatal nor would he now risk communicating the fact of his wife's flight to anyone till the inquest was over <\s>
<s> that morning he had risen early before the postman came had taken the first post letters from the box himself and though there had been none from irene he had made an opportunity of telling bilson that her mistress was at the sea he would probably he said be going down himself from saturday to monday <\s>
<s> this had given him time to breathe time to leave no stone unturned to find her <\s>
<s> but now cut off from taking steps by bosinney's death that strange death to think of which was like putting a hot iron to his heart like lifting a great weight from it he did not know how to pass his day and he wandered here and there through the streets looking at every face he met devoured by a hundred anxieties <\s>
<s> and as he wandered he thought of him who had finished his wandering his prowling and would never haunt his house again <\s>
<s> already in the afternoon he passed posters announcing the identity of the dead man and bought the papers to see what they said <\s>

<s> but now cut off from taking steps by bosinney's death that strange death to think of which was like putting a hot iron to his heart like lifting a great weight from it he did not know how to pass his day and he wandered here and there through the streets looking at every face he met devoured by a hundred anxieties <\s>
<s> and as he wandered he thought of him who had finished his wandering his prowling and would never haunt his house again <\s>
<s> already in the afternoon he passed posters announcing the identity of the dead man and bought the papers to see what they said <\s>
<s> he would stop their mouths if he could and he went into the city and was closeted with boulter for a long time <\s>
<s> on his way home passing the steps of jobson's about half past four he met george forsyte who held out an evening paper to soames saying here <\s>
<s> have you seen this about the poor buccaneer <\s>
<s> soames answered stonily yes <\s>
<s> george stared at him <\s>
<s> he had never liked soames he now held him responsible for bosinney's death <\s>
<s> and the thought of how to keep june's name out of the business kept whirring in his brain <\s>
<s> james had his son to support him <\s>
<s> why should he not send for jo <\s>
<s> taking out his card case he pencilled the following message come round at once <\s>
<s> i've sent the carriage for you <\s>
<s> on getting out he gave this card to his coachman telling him to drive as fast as possible to the hotch potch club and if mr <\s>
<s> jolyon forsyte were there to give him the card and bring him at once <\s>
<s> if not there yet he was to wait till he came <\s>
<s> he followed the others slowly up the steps leaning on his umbrella and stood a moment to get his breath <\s>
<s> the inspector said this is the mortuary sir <\s>
<s> but take your time <\s>
<s> in the bare white walled room empty of all but a streak of sunshine smeared along the dustless floor lay a form covered by a sheet <\s>
<s> with a huge steady hand the inspector took the hem and turned it back <\s>
<s> a sightless face gazed up at them and on either side of that sightless defiant face the three forsytes gazed down in each one of them the secret emotions fears and pity of his own nature rose and fell like the rising falling waves of life whose wash those white walls barred out now for ever from bosinney <\s>
<s> and in each one of them the trend of his nature the odd essential spring which moved him in fashions minutely unalterably different from those of every other human being forced him to a different attitude of thought <\s>
<s> far from the others yet inscrutably close each stood thus alone with death silent his eyes lowered <\s>
<s> the inspector asked softly you identify the gentleman sir <\s>
<s> old jolyon raised his head and nodded <\s>
<s> he looked at his brother opposite at that long lean figure brooding over the dead man with face dusky red and strained grey eyes and at the figure of soames white and still by his father's side <\s>
<s> and all that he had felt against those two was gone like smoke in the long white presence of death <\s>
<s> whence comes it how comes it death <\s>
<s> sudden reverse of all that goes before blind setting forth on a path that leads to where <\s>
<s> dark quenching of the fire <\s>
<s> the heavy brutal crushing out that all men must go through keeping their eyes clear and brave unto the end <\s>
<s> small and of no import insects though they are <\s>
<s> and across old jolyon's face there flitted a gleam for soames murmuring to the inspector crept noiselessly away <\s>
<s> then suddenly james raised his eyes <\s>
<s> there was a queer appeal in that suspicious troubled look i know i'm no match for you it seemed to say <\s>
<s> and hunting for handkerchief he wiped his brow then bending sorrowful and lank over the dead man he too turned and hurried out <\s>
<s> old jolyon stood still as death his eyes fixed on the body <\s>
<s> who shall tell of what he was thinking <\s>
<s> of himself when his hair was brown like the hair of that young fellow dead before him <\s>

<s> of that other woman <\s>
<s> of the strangeness and the pity of it <\s>
<s> and the irony inscrutable and bitter of that end <\s>
<s> there was no justice for men for they were ever in the dark <\s>
<s> or perhaps in his philosophy he thought better to be out of it all <\s>
<s> better to have done with it like this poor youth .... <\s>
<s> some one touched him on the arm <\s>
<s> a tear started up and wetted his eyelash <\s>
<s> well he said i'm no good here <\s>
<s> i'd better be going <\s>
<s> you'll come to me as soon as you can jo and with his head bowed he went away <\s>
<s> it was young jolyon's turn to take his stand beside the dead man round whose fallen body he seemed to see all the forsytes breathless and prostrated <\s>
<s> the stroke had fallen too swiftly <\s>
<s> the forces underlying every tragedy forces that take no denial working through cross currents to their ironical end had met and fused with a thunder clap flung out the victim and flattened to the ground all those that stood around <\s>
<s> or so at all events young jolyon seemed to see them lying around bosinney's body <\s>
<s> he asked the inspector to tell him what had happened and the latter like a man who does not every day get such a chance again detailed such facts as were known <\s>
<s> there's more here sir however he said than meets the eye <\s>
<s> i don't believe in suicide nor in pure accident myself <\s>
<s> it's more likely i think that he was suffering under great stress of mind and took no notice of things about him <\s>
<s> perhaps you can throw some light on these <\s>
<s> he took from his pocket a little packet and laid it on the table <\s>
<s> carefully undoing it he revealed a lady's handkerchief pinned through the folds with a pin of discoloured venetian gold the stone of which had fallen from the socket <\s>
<s> a scent of dried violets rose to young jolyon's nostrils <\s>
<s> found in his breast pocket said the inspector the name has been cut away <\s>
<s> young jolyon with difficulty answered i'm afraid i cannot help you <\s>
<s> but vividly there rose before him the face he had seen light up so tremulous and glad at bosinney's coming <\s>
<s> of her he thought more than of his own daughter more than of them all of her with the dark soft glance the delicate passive face waiting for the dead man waiting even at that moment perhaps still and patient in the sunlight <\s>
<s> he walked sorrowfully away from the hospital towards his father's house reflecting that this death would break up the forsyte family <\s>
<s> the stroke had indeed slipped past their defences into the very wood of their tree <\s>
<s> they might flourish to all appearance as before preserving a brave show before the eyes of london but the trunk was dead withered by the same flash that had stricken down bosinney <\s>
<s> and now the saplings would take its place each one a new custodian of the sense of property <\s>
<s> good forest of forsytes <\s>
<s> thought young jolyon soundest timber of our land <\s>
<s> concerning the cause of this death his family would doubtless reject with vigour the suspicion of suicide which was so compromising <\s>
<s> they would take it as an accident a stroke of fate <\s>
<s> in their hearts they would even feel it an intervention of providence a retribution had not bosinney endangered their two most priceless possessions the pocket and the hearth <\s>
<s> and they would talk of that unfortunate accident of young bosinney's but perhaps they would not talk silence might be better <\s>
<s> as for himself he regarded the bus driver's account of the accident as of very little value <\s>
<s> for no one so madly in love committed suicide for want of money nor was bosinney the sort of fellow to set much store by a financial crisis <\s>
<s> and so he too rejected this theory of suicide the dead man's face rose too clearly before him <\s>
<s> gone in the heyday of his summer and to believe thus that an accident had cut bosinney off in the full sweep of his passion was more than ever pitiful to young jolyon <\s>
<s> then came a vision of soames home as it now was and must be hereafter <\s>
<s> the streak of lightning had flashed its clear uncanny gleam on bare bones with grinning spaces between the disguising flesh was gone .... <\s>

<s> i've told poor little june <\s>
<s> but that's not all of it <\s>

<s> chapter ix irene's return after leaving james and old jolyon in the mortuary of the hospital soames hurried aimlessly along the streets <\s>
<s> the tragic event of bosinney's death altered the complexion of everything <\s>
<s> there was no longer the same feeling that to lose a minute would be fatal nor would he now risk communicating the fact of his wife's flight to anyone till the inquest was over <\s>
<s> that morning he had risen early before the postman came had taken the first post letters from the box himself and though there had been none from irene he had made an opportunity of telling bilson that her mistress was at the sea he would probably he said be going down himself from saturday to monday <\s>
<s> this had given him time to breathe time to leave no stone unturned to find her <\s>
<s> but now cut off from taking steps by bosinney's death that strange death to think of which was like putting a hot iron to his heart like lifting a great weight from it he did not know how to pass his day and he wandered here and there through the streets looking at every face he met devoured by a hundred anxieties <\s>
<s> and as he wandered he thought of him who had finished his wandering his prowling and would never haunt his house again <\s>
<s> already in the afternoon he passed posters announcing the identity of the dead man and bought the papers to see what they said <\s>
<s> he would stop their mouths if he could and he went into the city and was closeted with boulter for a long time <\s>
<s> on his way home passing the steps of jobson's about half past four he met george forsyte who held out an evening paper to soames saying here <\s>
<s> have you seen this about the poor buccaneer <\s>
<s> soames answered stonily yes <\s>
<s> george stared at him <\s>
<s> he had never liked soames he now held him responsible for bosinney's death <\s>
<s> and the thought of how to keep june's name out of the business kept whirring in his brain <\s>
<s> james had his son to support him <\s>
<s> why should he not send for jo <\s>
<s> taking out his card case he pencilled the following message come round at once <\s>
<s> i've sent the carriage for you <\s>
<s> on getting out he gave this card to his coachman telling him to drive as fast as possible to the hotch potch club and if mr <\s>
<s> jolyon forsyte were there to give him the card and bring him at once <\s>
<s> if not there yet he was to wait till he came <\s>
<s> he followed the others slowly up the steps leaning on his umbrella and stood a moment to get his breath <\s>
<s> the inspector said this is the mortuary sir <\s>
<s> but take your time <\s>
<s> in the bare white walled room empty of all but a streak of sunshine smeared along the dustless floor lay a form covered by a sheet <\s>
<s> with a huge steady hand the inspector took the hem and turned it back <\s>
<s> a sightless face gazed up at them and on either side of that sightless defiant face the three forsytes gazed down in each one of them the secret emotions fears and pity of his own nature rose and fell like the rising falling waves of life whose wash those white walls barred out now for ever from bosinney <\s>
<s> and in each one of them the trend of his nature the odd essential spring which moved him in fashions minutely unalterably different from those of every other human being forced him to a different attitude of thought <\s>
<s> far from the others yet inscrutably close each stood thus alone with death silent his eyes lowered <\s>
<s> the inspector asked softly you identify the gentleman sir <\s>
<s> old jolyon raised his head and nodded <\s>
<s> he looked at his brother opposite at that long lean figure brooding over the dead man with face dusky red and strained grey eyes and at the figure of soames white and still by his father's side <\s>
<s> and all that he had felt against those two was gone like smoke in the long white presence of death <\s>
<s> whence comes it how comes it death <\s>
<s> sudden reverse of all that goes before blind setting forth on a path that leads to where <\s>
<s> dark quenching of the fire <\s>
<s> the heavy brutal crushing out that all men must go through keeping their eyes clear and brave unto the end <\s>
<s> small and of no import insects though they are <\s>
<s> and across old jolyon's face there flitted a gleam for soames murmuring to the inspector crept noiselessly away <\s>
<s> then suddenly james raised his eyes <\s>
<s> there was a queer appeal in that suspicious troubled look i know i'm no match for you it seemed to say <\s>
<s> and hunting for handkerchief he wiped his brow then bending sorrowful and lank over the dead man he too turned and hurried out <\s>
<s> old jolyon stood still as death his eyes fixed on the body <\s>
<s> who shall tell of what he was thinking <\s>
<s> of himself when his hair was brown like the hair of that young fellow dead before him <\s>
<s> of himself with his battle just beginning the long long battle he had loved the battle that was over for this young man almost before it had begun <\s>
<s> of his grand daughter with her broken hopes <\s>
<s> of that other woman <\s>
<s> of the strangeness and the pity of it <\s>
<s> and the irony inscrutable and bitter of that end <\s>
<s> there was no justice for men for they were ever in the dark <\s>
<s> or perhaps in his philosophy he thought better to be out of it all <\s>
<s> better to have done with it like this poor youth .... <\s>
<s> some one touched him on the arm <\s>
<s> a tear started up and wetted his eyelash <\s>
<s> well he said i'm no good here <\s>
<s> i'd better be going <\s>
<s> you'll come to me as soon as you can jo and with his head bowed he went away <\s>
<s> it was young jolyon's turn to take his stand beside the dead man round whose fallen body he seemed to see all the forsytes breathless and prostrated <\s>
<s> the stroke had fallen too swiftly <\s>
<s> the forces underlying every tragedy forces that take no denial working through cross currents to their ironical end had met and fused with a thunder clap flung out the victim and flattened to the ground all those that stood around <\s>
<s> or so at all events young jolyon seemed to see them lying around bosinney's body <\s>
<s> he asked the inspector to tell him what had happened and the latter like a man who does not every day get such a chance again detailed such facts as were known <\s>
<s> there's more here sir however he said than meets the eye <\s>
<s> i don't believe in suicide nor in pure accident myself <\s>
<s> it's more likely i think that he was suffering under great stress of mind and took no notice of things about him <\s>
<s> perhaps you can throw some light on these <\s>
<s> he took from his pocket a little packet and laid it on the table <\s>
<s> carefully undoing it he revealed a lady's handkerchief pinned through the folds with a pin of discoloured venetian gold the stone of which had fallen from the socket <\s>
<s> a scent of dried violets rose to young jolyon's nostrils <\s>
<s> found in his breast pocket said the inspector the name has been cut away <\s>
<s> young jolyon with difficulty answered i'm afraid i cannot help you <\s>
<s> but vividly there rose before him the face he had seen light up so tremulous and glad at bosinney's coming <\s>
<s> of her he thought more than of his own daughter more than of them all of her with the dark soft glance the delicate passive face waiting for the dead man waiting even at that moment perhaps still and patient in the sunlight <\s>
<s> he walked sorrowfully away from the hospital towards his father's house reflecting that this death would break up the forsyte family <\s>
<s> the stroke had indeed slipped past their defences into the very wood of their tree <\s>
<s> they might flourish to all appearance as before preserving a brave show before the eyes of london but the trunk was dead withered by the same flash that had stricken down bosinney <\s>
<s> and now the saplings would take its place each one a new custodian of the sense of property <\s>
<s> good forest of forsytes <\s>
<s> thought young jolyon soundest timber of our land <\s>
<s> concerning the cause of this death his family would doubtless reject with vigour the suspicion of suicide which was so compromising <\s>
<s> they would take it as an accident a stroke of fate <\s>
<s> in their hearts they would even feel it an intervention of providence a retribution had not bosinney endangered their two most priceless possessions the pocket and the hearth <\s>
<s> and they would talk of that unfortunate accident of young bosinney's but perhaps they would not talk silence might be better <\s>
<s> as for himself he regarded the bus driver's account of the accident as of very little value <\s>
<s> for no one so madly in love committed suicide for want of money nor was bosinney the sort of fellow to set much store by a financial crisis <\s>
<s> and so he too rejected this theory of suicide the dead man's face rose too clearly before him <\s>

<s> and now the saplings would take its place each one a new custodian of the sense of property <\s>
<s> good forest of forsytes <\s>
<s> thought young jolyon soundest timber of our land <\s>
<s> concerning the cause of this death his family would doubtless reject with vigour the suspicion of suicide which was so compromising <\s>
<s> they would take it as an accident a stroke of fate <\s>
<s> in their hearts they would even feel it an intervention of providence a retribution had not bosinney endangered their two most priceless possessions the pocket and the hearth <\s>
<s> and they would talk of that unfortunate accident of young bosinney's but perhaps they would not talk silence might be better <\s>
<s> as for himself he regarded the bus driver's account of the accident as of very little value <\s>
<s> for no one so madly in love committed suicide for want of money nor was bosinney the sort of fellow to set much store by a financial crisis <\s>
<s> and so he too rejected this theory of suicide the dead man's face rose too clearly before him <\s>
<s> gone in the heyday of his summer and to believe thus that an accident had cut bosinney off in the full sweep of his passion was more than ever pitiful to young jolyon <\s>
<s> then came a vision of soames home as it now was and must be hereafter <\s>
<s> the streak of lightning had flashed its clear uncanny gleam on bare bones with grinning spaces between the disguising flesh was gone .... <\s>
<s> in the dining room at stanhope gate old jolyon was sitting alone when his son came in <\s>
<s> he looked very wan in his great armchair <\s>
<s> and his eyes travelling round the walls with their pictures of still life and the masterpiece dutch fishing boats at sunset seemed as though passing their gaze over his life with its hopes its gains its achievements <\s>
<s> he said is that you <\s>
<s> i've told poor little june <\s>
<s> but that's not all of it <\s>
<s> are you going to soames <\s>
<s> she's brought it on herself i suppose but somehow i can't bear to think of her shut up there and all alone <\s>
<s> and holding up his thin veined hand he clenched it <\s>
<s> chapter ix irene's return after leaving james and old jolyon in the mortuary of the hospital soames hurried aimlessly along the streets <\s>
<s> the tragic event of bosinney's death altered the complexion of everything <\s>
<s> there was no longer the same feeling that to lose a minute would be fatal nor would he now risk communicating the fact of his wife's flight to anyone till the inquest was over <\s>
<s> that morning he had risen early before the postman came had taken the first post letters from the box himself and though there had been none from irene he had made an opportunity of telling bilson that her mistress was at the sea he would probably he said be going down himself from saturday to monday <\s>
<s> this had given him time to breathe time to leave no stone unturned to find her <\s>
<s> but now cut off from taking steps by bosinney's death that strange death to think of which was like putting a hot iron to his heart like lifting a great weight from it he did not know how to pass his day and he wandered here and there through the streets looking at every face he met devoured by a hundred anxieties <\s>
<s> and as he wandered he thought of him who had finished his wandering his prowling and would never haunt his house again <\s>
<s> already in the afternoon he passed posters announcing the identity of the dead man and bought the papers to see what they said <\s>
<s> he would stop their mouths if he could and he went into the city and was closeted with boulter for a long time <\s>
<s> on his way home passing the steps of jobson's about half past four he met george forsyte who held out an evening paper to soames saying here <\s>
<s> have you seen this about the poor buccaneer <\s>
<s> soames answered stonily yes <\s>
<s> george stared at him <\s>
<s> he had never liked soames he now held him responsible for bosinney's death <\s>
<s> and the thought of how to keep june's name out of the business kept whirring in his brain <\s>
<s> james had his son to support him <\s>
<s> why should he not send for jo <\s>
<s> taking out his card case he pencilled the following message come round at once <\s>
<s> i've sent the carriage for you <\s>
<s> on getting out he gave this card to his coachman telling him to drive as fast as possible to the hotch potch club and if mr <\s>
<s> jolyon forsyte were there to give him the card and bring him at once <\s>
<s> if not there yet he was to wait till he came <\s>
<s> he followed the others slowly up the steps leaning on his umbrella and stood a moment to get his breath <\s>
<s> the inspector said this is the mortuary sir <\s>
<s> but take your time <\s>
<s> in the bare white walled room empty of all but a streak of sunshine smeared along the dustless floor lay a form covered by a sheet <\s>
<s> with a huge steady hand the inspector took the hem and turned it back <\s>
<s> a sightless face gazed up at them and on either side of that sightless defiant face the three forsytes gazed down in each one of them the secret emotions fears and pity of his own nature rose and fell like the rising falling waves of life whose wash those white walls barred out now for ever from bosinney <\s>
<s> and in each one of them the trend of his nature the odd essential spring which moved him in fashions minutely unalterably different from those of every other human being forced him to a different attitude of thought <\s>
<s> far from the others yet inscrutably close each stood thus alone with death silent his eyes lowered <\s>
<s> the inspector asked softly you identify the gentleman sir <\s>
<s> old jolyon raised his head and nodded <\s>
<s> he looked at his brother opposite at that long lean figure brooding over the dead man with face dusky red and strained grey eyes and at the figure of soames white and still by his father's side <\s>
<s> and all that he had felt against those two was gone like smoke in the long white presence of death <\s>
<s> whence comes it how comes it death <\s>
<s> sudden reverse of all that goes before blind setting forth on a path that leads to where <\s>
<s> dark quenching of the fire <\s>
<s> the heavy brutal crushing out that all men must go through keeping their eyes clear and brave unto the end <\s>
<s> small and of no import insects though they are <\s>

<s> there was a queer appeal in that suspicious troubled look i know i'm no match for you it seemed to say <\s>
<s> and hunting for handkerchief he wiped his brow then bending sorrowful and lank over the dead man he too turned and hurried out <\s>
<s> old jolyon stood still as death his eyes fixed on the body <\s>
<s> who shall tell of what he was thinking <\s>
<s> of himself when his hair was brown like the hair of that young fellow dead before him <\s>

<s> of that other woman <\s>
<s> of the strangeness and the pity of it <\s>
<s> and the irony inscrutable and bitter of that end <\s>
<s> there was no justice for men for they were ever in the dark <\s>
<s> or perhaps in his philosophy he thought better to be out of it all <\s>
<s> better to have done with it like this poor youth .... <\s>

<s> well he said i'm no good here <\s>
<s> i'd better be going <\s>
<s> you'll come to me as soon as you can jo and with his head bowed he went away <\s>
<s> it was young jolyon's turn to take his stand beside the dead man round whose fallen body he seemed to see all the forsytes breathless and prostrated <\s>
<s> the stroke had fallen too swiftly <\s>

<s> or so at all events young jolyon seemed to see them lying around bosinney's body <\s>

<s> the stroke had indeed slipped past their defences into the very wood of their tree <\s>

<s> thought young jolyon soundest timber of our land <\s>
<s> concerning the cause of this death his family would doubtless reject with vigour the suspicion of suicide which was so compromising <\s>

<s> in their hearts they would even feel it an intervention of providence a retribution had not bosinney endangered their two most priceless possessions the pocket and the hearth <\s>
<s> and they would talk of that unfortunate accident of young bosinney's but perhaps they would not talk silence might be better <\s>
<s> as for himself he regarded the bus driver's account of the accident as of very little value <\s>
<s> for no one so madly in love committed suicide for want of money nor was bosinney the sort of fellow to set much store by a financial crisis <\s>
<s> and so he too rejected this theory of suicide the dead man's face rose too clearly before him <\s>

<s> chapter ix irene's return after leaving james and old jolyon in the mortuary of the hospital soames hurried aimlessly along the streets <\s>
<s> the tragic event of bosinney's death altered the complexion of everything <\s>
<s> there was no longer the same feeling that to lose a minute would be fatal nor would he now risk communicating the fact of his wife's flight to anyone till the inquest was over <\s>
<s> that morning he had risen early before the postman came had taken the first post letters from the box himself and though there had been none from irene he had made an opportunity of telling bilson that her mistress was at the sea he would probably he said be going down himself from saturday to monday <\s>
<s> this had given him time to breathe time to leave no stone unturned to find her <\s>
<s> but now cut off from taking steps by bosinney's death that strange death to think of which was like putting a hot iron to his heart like lifting a great weight from it he did not know how to pass his day and he wandered here and there through the streets looking at every face he met devoured by a hundred anxieties <\s>
<s> and as he wandered he thought of him who had finished his wandering his prowling and would never haunt his house again <\s>
<s> already in the afternoon he passed posters announcing the identity of the dead man and bought the papers to see what they said <\s>
<s> he would stop their mouths if he could and he went into the city and was closeted with boulter for a long time <\s>
<s> on his way home passing the steps of jobson's about half past four he met george forsyte who held out an evening paper to soames saying here <\s>
<s> have you seen this about the poor buccaneer <\s>
<s> soames answered stonily yes <\s>
<s> george stared at him <\s>
<s> he had never liked soames he now held him responsible for bosinney's death <\s>

<s> and in each one of them the trend of his nature the odd essential spring which moved him in fashions minutely unalterably different from those of every other human being forced him to a different attitude of thought <\s>
<s> far from the others yet inscrutably close each stood thus alone with death silent his eyes lowered <\s>

<s> chapter ix irene's return after leaving james and old jolyon in the mortuary of the hospital soames hurried aimlessly along the streets <\s>
<s> the tragic event of bosinney's death altered the complexion of everything <\s>
<s> there was no longer the same feeling that to lose a minute would be fatal nor would he now risk communicating the fact of his wife's flight to anyone till the inquest was over <\s>
<s> that morning he had risen early before the postman came had taken the first post letters from the box himself and though there had been none from irene he had made an opportunity of telling bilson that her mistress was at the sea he would probably he said be going down himself from saturday to monday <\s>
<s> this had given him time to breathe time to leave no stone unturned to find her <\s>
<s> but now cut off from taking steps by bosinney's death that strange death to think of which was like putting a hot iron to his heart like lifting a great weight from it he did not know how to pass his day and he wandered here and there through the streets looking at every face he met devoured by a hundred anxieties <\s>
<s> and as he wandered he thought of him who had finished his wandering his prowling and would never haunt his house again <\s>
<s> already in the afternoon he passed posters announcing the identity of the dead man and bought the papers to see what they said <\s>
<s> he would stop their mouths if he could and he went into the city and was closeted with boulter for a long time <\s>

<s> that morning he had risen early before the postman came had taken the first post letters from the box himself and though there had been none from irene he had made an opportunity of telling bilson that her mistress was at the sea he would probably he said be going down himself from saturday to monday <\s>
<s> this had given him time to breathe time to leave no stone unturned to find her <\s>
<s> but now cut off from taking steps by bosinney's death that strange death to think of which was like putting a hot iron to his heart like lifting a great weight from it he did not know how to pass his day and he wandered here and there through the streets looking at every face he met devoured by a hundred anxieties <\s>
<s> and as he wandered he thought of him who had finished his wandering his prowling and would never haunt his house again <\s>
<s> already in the afternoon he passed posters announcing the identity of the dead man and bought the papers to see what they said <\s>

<s> but take your time <\s>
<s> in the bare white walled room empty of all but a streak of sunshine smeared along the dustless floor lay a form covered by a sheet <\s>
<s> with a huge steady hand the inspector took the hem and turned it back <\s>
<s> a sightless face gazed up at them and on either side of that sightless defiant face the three forsytes gazed down in each one of them the secret emotions fears and pity of his own nature rose and fell like the rising falling waves of life whose wash those white walls barred out now for ever from bosinney <\s>
<s> and in each one of them the trend of his nature the odd essential spring which moved him in fashions minutely unalterably different from those of every other human being forced him to a different attitude of thought <\s>
<s> far from the others yet inscrutably close each stood thus alone with death silent his eyes lowered <\s>
<s> the inspector asked softly you identify the gentleman sir <\s>
<s> old jolyon raised his head and nodded <\s>
<s> he looked at his brother opposite at that long lean figure brooding over the dead man with face dusky red and strained grey eyes and at the figure of soames white and still by his father's side <\s>
<s> and all that he had felt against those two was gone like smoke in the long white presence of death <\s>

<s> sudden reverse of all that goes before blind setting forth on a path that leads to where <\s>
<s> dark quenching of the fire <\s>
<s> the heavy brutal crushing out that all men must go through keeping their eyes clear and brave unto the end <\s>
<s> small and of no import insects though they are <\s>

<s> there was a queer appeal in that suspicious troubled look i know i'm no match for you it seemed to say <\s>

<s> of that other woman <\s>

<s> you'll come to me as soon as you can jo and with his head bowed he went away <\s>
<s> it was young jolyon's turn to take his stand beside the dead man round whose fallen body he seemed to see all the forsytes breathless and prostrated <\s>
<s> the stroke had fallen too swiftly <\s>
<s> the forces underlying every tragedy forces that take no denial working through cross currents to their ironical end had met and fused with a thunder clap flung out the victim and flattened to the ground all those that stood around <\s>
<s> or so at all events young jolyon seemed to see them lying around bosinney's body <\s>
<s> he asked the inspector to tell him what had happened and the latter like a man who does not every day get such a chance again detailed such facts as were known <\s>
<s> there's more here sir however he said than meets the eye <\s>
<s> i don't believe in suicide nor in pure accident myself <\s>
<s> it's more likely i think that he was suffering under great stress of mind and took no notice of things about him <\s>
<s> perhaps you can throw some light on these <\s>
<s> he took from his pocket a little packet and laid it on the table <\s>

<s> a scent of dried violets rose to young jolyon's nostrils <\s>
<s> found in his breast pocket said the inspector the name has been cut away <\s>
<s> young jolyon with difficulty answered i'm afraid i cannot help you <\s>
<s> but vividly there rose before him the face he had seen light up so tremulous and glad at bosinney's coming <\s>
<s> of her he thought more than of his own daughter more than of them all of her with the dark soft glance the delicate passive face waiting for the dead man waiting even at that moment perhaps still and patient in the sunlight <\s>
<s> he walked sorrowfully away from the hospital towards his father's house reflecting that this death would break up the forsyte family <\s>
<s> the stroke had indeed slipped past their defences into the very wood of their tree <\s>
<s> they might flourish to all appearance as before preserving a brave show before the eyes of london but the trunk was dead withered by the same flash that had stricken down bosinney <\s>
<s> and now the saplings would take its place each one a new custodian of the sense of property <\s>
<s> good forest of forsytes <\s>
<s> thought young jolyon soundest timber of our land <\s>
<s> concerning the cause of this death his family would doubtless reject with vigour the suspicion of suicide which was so compromising <\s>
<s> they would take it as an accident a stroke of fate <\s>
<s> in their hearts they would even feel it an intervention of providence a retribution had not bosinney endangered their two most priceless possessions the pocket and the hearth <\s>
<s> and they would talk of that unfortunate accident of young bosinney's but perhaps they would not talk silence might be better <\s>
<s> as for himself he regarded the bus driver's account of the accident as of very little value <\s>
<s> for no one so madly in love committed suicide for want of money nor was bosinney the sort of fellow to set much store by a financial crisis <\s>
<s> and so he too rejected this theory of suicide the dead man's face rose too clearly before him <\s>
<s> gone in the heyday of his summer and to believe thus that an accident had cut bosinney off in the full sweep of his passion was more than ever pitiful to young jolyon <\s>
<s> then came a vision of soames home as it now was and must be hereafter <\s>

<s> chapter ix irene's return after leaving james and old jolyon in the mortuary of the hospital soames hurried aimlessly along the streets <\s>
<s> the tragic event of bosinney's death altered the complexion of everything <\s>
<s> there was no longer the same feeling that to lose a minute would be fatal nor would he now risk communicating the fact of his wife's flight to anyone till the inquest was over <\s>
<s> that morning he had risen early before the postman came had taken the first post letters from the box himself and though there had been none from irene he had made an opportunity of telling bilson that her mistress was at the sea he would probably he said be going down himself from saturday to monday <\s>
<s> this had given him time to breathe time to leave no stone unturned to find her <\s>
<s> but now cut off from taking steps by bosinney's death that strange death to think of which was like putting a hot iron to his heart like lifting a great weight from it he did not know how to pass his day and he wandered here and there through the streets looking at every face he met devoured by a hundred anxieties <\s>
<s> and as he wandered he thought of him who had finished his wandering his prowling and would never haunt his house again <\s>
<s> already in the afternoon he passed posters announcing the identity of the dead man and bought the papers to see what they said <\s>
<s> he would stop their mouths if he could and he went into the city and was closeted with boulter for a long time <\s>
<s> on his way home passing the steps of jobson's about half past four he met george forsyte who held out an evening paper to soames saying here <\s>

<s> george stared at him <\s>

<s> he would stop their mouths if he could and he went into the city and was closeted with boulter for a long time <\s>
<s> on his way home passing the steps of jobson's about half past four he met george forsyte who held out an evening paper to soames saying here <\s>
<s> have you seen this about the poor buccaneer <\s>
<s> soames answered stonily yes <\s>
<s> george stared at him <\s>
<s> he had never liked soames he now held him responsible for bosinney's death <\s>
<s> and the thought of how to keep june's name out of the business kept whirring in his brain <\s>
<s> james had his son to support him <\s>
<s> why should he not send for jo <\s>
<s> taking out his card case he pencilled the following message come round at once <\s>
<s> i've sent the carriage for you <\s>
<s> on getting out he gave this card to his coachman telling him to drive as fast as possible to the hotch potch club and if mr <\s>
<s> jolyon forsyte were there to give him the card and bring him at once <\s>
<s> if not there yet he was to wait till he came <\s>
<s> he followed the others slowly up the steps leaning on his umbrella and stood a moment to get his breath <\s>
<s> the inspector said this is the mortuary sir <\s>
<s> but take your time <\s>
<s> in the bare white walled room empty of all but a streak of sunshine smeared along the dustless floor lay a form covered by a sheet <\s>
<s> with a huge steady hand the inspector took the hem and turned it back <\s>
<s> a sightless face gazed up at them and on either side of that sightless defiant face the three forsytes gazed down in each one of them the secret emotions fears and pity of his own nature rose and fell like the rising falling waves of life whose wash those white walls barred out now for ever from bosinney <\s>
<s> and in each one of them the trend of his nature the odd essential spring which moved him in fashions minutely unalterably different from those of every other human being forced him to a different attitude of thought <\s>
<s> far from the others yet inscrutably close each stood thus alone with death silent his eyes lowered <\s>
<s> the inspector asked softly you identify the gentleman sir <\s>
<s> old jolyon raised his head and nodded <\s>
<s> he looked at his brother opposite at that long lean figure brooding over the dead man with face dusky red and strained grey eyes and at the figure of soames white and still by his father's side <\s>
<s> and all that he had felt against those two was gone like smoke in the long white presence of death <\s>
<s> whence comes it how comes it death <\s>
<s> sudden reverse of all that goes before blind setting forth on a path that leads to where <\s>
<s> dark quenching of the fire <\s>
<s> the heavy brutal crushing out that all men must go through keeping their eyes clear and brave unto the end <\s>
<s> small and of no import insects though they are <\s>

<s> then suddenly james raised his eyes <\s>
<s> there was a queer appeal in that suspicious troubled look i know i'm no match for you it seemed to say <\s>

<s> old jolyon stood still as death his eyes fixed on the body <\s>

<s> i'd better be going <\s>
<s> you'll come to me as soon as you can jo and with his head bowed he went away <\s>
<s> it was young jolyon's turn to take his stand beside the dead man round whose fallen body he seemed to see all the forsytes breathless and prostrated <\s>
<s> the stroke had fallen too swiftly <\s>
<s> the forces underlying every tragedy forces that take no denial working through cross currents to their ironical end had met and fused with a thunder clap flung out the victim and flattened to the ground all those that stood around <\s>
<s> or so at all events young jolyon seemed to see them lying around bosinney's body <\s>
<s> he asked the inspector to tell him what had happened and the latter like a man who does not every day get such a chance again detailed such facts as were known <\s>
<s> there's more here sir however he said than meets the eye <\s>
<s> i don't believe in suicide nor in pure accident myself <\s>
<s> it's more likely i think that he was suffering under great stress of mind and took no notice of things about him <\s>
<s> perhaps you can throw some light on these <\s>
<s> he took from his pocket a little packet and laid it on the table <\s>

<s> a scent of dried violets rose to young jolyon's nostrils <\s>
<s> found in his breast pocket said the inspector the name has been cut away <\s>
<s> young jolyon with difficulty answered i'm afraid i cannot help you <\s>
<s> but vividly there rose before him the face he had seen light up so tremulous and glad at bosinney's coming <\s>
<s> of her he thought more than of his own daughter more than of them all of her with the dark soft glance the delicate passive face waiting for the dead man waiting even at that moment perhaps still and patient in the sunlight <\s>
<s> he walked sorrowfully away from the hospital towards his father's house reflecting that this death would break up the forsyte family <\s>
<s> the stroke had indeed slipped past their defences into the very wood of their tree <\s>
<s> they might flourish to all appearance as before preserving a brave show before the eyes of london but the trunk was dead withered by the same flash that had stricken down bosinney <\s>
<s> and now the saplings would take its place each one a new custodian of the sense of property <\s>
<s> good forest of forsytes <\s>
<s> thought young jolyon soundest timber of our land <\s>
<s> concerning the cause of this death his family would doubtless reject with vigour the suspicion of suicide which was so compromising <\s>
<s> they would take it as an accident a stroke of fate <\s>
<s> in their hearts they would even feel it an intervention of providence a retribution had not bosinney endangered their two most priceless possessions the pocket and the hearth <\s>
<s> and they would talk of that unfortunate accident of young bosinney's but perhaps they would not talk silence might be better <\s>
<s> as for himself he regarded the bus driver's account of the accident as of very little value <\s>
<s> for no one so madly in love committed suicide for want of money nor was bosinney the sort of fellow to set much store by a financial crisis <\s>
<s> and so he too rejected this theory of suicide the dead man's face rose too clearly before him <\s>
<s> gone in the heyday of his summer and to believe thus that an accident had cut bosinney off in the full sweep of his passion was more than ever pitiful to young jolyon <\s>
<s> then came a vision of soames home as it now was and must be hereafter <\s>

<s> chapter ix irene's return after leaving james and old jolyon in the mortuary of the hospital soames hurried aimlessly along the streets <\s>

<s> chapter ix irene's return after leaving james and old jolyon in the mortuary of the hospital soames hurried aimlessly along the streets <\s>
<s> the tragic event of bosinney's death altered the complexion of everything <\s>
<s> there was no longer the same feeling that to lose a minute would be fatal nor would he now risk communicating the fact of his wife's flight to anyone till the inquest was over <\s>
<s> that morning he had risen early before the postman came had taken the first post letters from the box himself and though there had been none from irene he had made an opportunity of telling bilson that her mistress was at the sea he would probably he said be going down himself from saturday to monday <\s>
<s> this had given him time to breathe time to leave no stone unturned to find her <\s>
<s> but now cut off from taking steps by bosinney's death that strange death to think of which was like putting a hot iron to his heart like lifting a great weight from it he did not know how to pass his day and he wandered here and there through the streets looking at every face he met devoured by a hundred anxieties <\s>
<s> and as he wandered he thought of him who had finished his wandering his prowling and would never haunt his house again <\s>
<s> already in the afternoon he passed posters announcing the identity of the dead man and bought the papers to see what they said <\s>
<s> he would stop their mouths if he could and he went into the city and was closeted with boulter for a long time <\s>
<s> on his way home passing the steps of jobson's about half past four he met george forsyte who held out an evening paper to soames saying here <\s>
<s> have you seen this about the poor buccaneer <\s>
<s> soames answered stonily yes <\s>
<s> george stared at him <\s>
<s> he had never liked soames he now held him responsible for bosinney's death <\s>
<s> and the thought of how to keep june's name out of the business kept whirring in his brain <\s>
<s> james had his son to support him <\s>
<s> why should he not send for jo <\s>
<s> taking out his card case he pencilled the following message come round at once <\s>
<s> i've sent the carriage for you <\s>
<s> on getting out he gave this card to his coachman telling him to drive as fast as possible to the hotch potch club and if mr <\s>
<s> jolyon forsyte were there to give him the card and bring him at once <\s>
<s> if not there yet he was to wait till he came <\s>
<s> he followed the others slowly up the steps leaning on his umbrella and stood a moment to get his breath <\s>
<s> the inspector said this is the mortuary sir <\s>
<s> but take your time <\s>
<s> in the bare white walled room empty of all but a streak of sunshine smeared along the dustless floor lay a form covered by a sheet <\s>
<s> with a huge steady hand the inspector took the hem and turned it back <\s>
<s> a sightless face gazed up at them and on either side of that sightless defiant face the three forsytes gazed down in each one of them the secret emotions fears and pity of his own nature rose and fell like the rising falling waves of life whose wash those white walls barred out now for ever from bosinney <\s>
<s> and in each one of them the trend of his nature the odd essential spring which moved him in fashions minutely unalterably different from those of every other human being forced him to a different attitude of thought <\s>
<s> far from the others yet inscrutably close each stood thus alone with death silent his eyes lowered <\s>
<s> the inspector asked softly you identify the gentleman sir <\s>
<s> old jolyon raised his head and nodded <\s>
<s> he looked at his brother opposite at that long lean figure brooding over the dead man with face dusky red and strained grey eyes and at the figure of soames white and still by his father's side <\s>
<s> and all that he had felt against those two was gone like smoke in the long white presence of death <\s>
<s> whence comes it how comes it death <\s>
<s> sudden reverse of all that goes before blind setting forth on a path that leads to where <\s>
<s> dark quenching of the fire <\s>
<s> the heavy brutal crushing out that all men must go through keeping their eyes clear and brave unto the end <\s>
<s> small and of no import insects though they are <\s>
<s> and across old jolyon's face there flitted a gleam for soames murmuring to the inspector crept noiselessly away <\s>
<s> then suddenly james raised his eyes <\s>
<s> there was a queer appeal in that suspicious troubled look i know i'm no match for you it seemed to say <\s>
<s> and hunting for handkerchief he wiped his brow then bending sorrowful and lank over the dead man he too turned and hurried out <\s>
<s> old jolyon stood still as death his eyes fixed on the body <\s>
<s> who shall tell of what he was thinking <\s>
<s> of himself when his hair was brown like the hair of that young fellow dead before him <\s>
<s> of himself with his battle just beginning the long long battle he had loved the battle that was over for this young man almost before it had begun <\s>

<s> of that other woman <\s>
<s> of the strangeness and the pity of it <\s>
<s> and the irony inscrutable and bitter of that end <\s>
<s> there was no justice for men for they were ever in the dark <\s>
<s> or perhaps in his philosophy he thought better to be out of it all <\s>
<s> better to have done with it like this poor youth .... <\s>
<s> some one touched him on the arm <\s>
<s> a tear started up and wetted his eyelash <\s>
<s> well he said i'm no good here <\s>
<s> i'd better be going <\s>
<s> you'll come to me as soon as you can jo and with his head bowed he went away <\s>
<s> it was young jolyon's turn to take his stand beside the dead man round whose fallen body he seemed to see all the forsytes breathless and prostrated <\s>
<s> the stroke had fallen too swiftly <\s>
<s> the forces underlying every tragedy forces that take no denial working through cross currents to their ironical end had met and fused with a thunder clap flung out the victim and flattened to the ground all those that stood around <\s>
<s> or so at all events young jolyon seemed to see them lying around bosinney's body <\s>
<s> he asked the inspector to tell him what had happened and the latter like a man who does not every day get such a chance again detailed such facts as were known <\s>
<s> there's more here sir however he said than meets the eye <\s>
<s> i don't believe in suicide nor in pure accident myself <\s>
<s> it's more likely i think that he was suffering under great stress of mind and took no notice of things about him <\s>
<s> perhaps you can throw some light on these <\s>
<s> he took from his pocket a little packet and laid it on the table <\s>

<s> a scent of dried violets rose to young jolyon's nostrils <\s>
<s> found in his breast pocket said the inspector the name has been cut away <\s>
<s> young jolyon with difficulty answered i'm afraid i cannot help you <\s>
<s> but vividly there rose before him the face he had seen light up so tremulous and glad at bosinney's coming <\s>

<s> he walked sorrowfully away from the hospital towards his father's house reflecting that this death would break up the forsyte family <\s>
<s> the stroke had indeed slipped past their defences into the very wood of their tree <\s>
<s> they might flourish to all appearance as before preserving a brave show before the eyes of london but the trunk was dead withered by the same flash that had stricken down bosinney <\s>
<s> and now the saplings would take its place each one a new custodian of the sense of property <\s>
<s> good forest of forsytes <\s>
<s> thought young jolyon soundest timber of our land <\s>
<s> concerning the cause of this death his family would doubtless reject with vigour the suspicion of suicide which was so compromising <\s>
<s> they would take it as an accident a stroke of fate <\s>
<s> in their hearts they would even feel it an intervention of providence a retribution had not bosinney endangered their two most priceless possessions the pocket and the hearth <\s>
<s> and they would talk of that unfortunate accident of young bosinney's but perhaps they would not talk silence might be better <\s>
<s> as for himself he regarded the bus driver's account of the accident as of very little value <\s>
<s> for no one so madly in love committed suicide for want of money nor was bosinney the sort of fellow to set much store by a financial crisis <\s>
<s> and so he too rejected this theory of suicide the dead man's face rose too clearly before him <\s>
